My wife and I have been customers at Airport Motors for more than 15 years. We've had at least 25 repairs done there. Jeff has always done an excellent job at a reasonable cost. He and his sons are 100% honest and are excellent mechanics. Just today (when I took the car in for a starting problem) they found a metal flap under our car that has been rattling for 3 months and bent it back so it doesn't rattle anymore. What a relief! Everyone we've talked to that uses Airport Motors has said the same, so I don't know where the negative reviews above are coming from. < Text>
I was wondering what to eat when I spotted the Deli and Bagel Cafe and decided to give it a try.  It's a small independent place in a strip mall with a few tables inside and a few more outside.  From the menus on the walls it looked like they did a big breakfast business but it was almost noon so I ordered a sandwich.  I got a chicken salad sandwich and ate it in my car.  The chicken salad was fresh and tasty and the bread was a match for the moist filling not falling apart half way through like a cheap supermarket bread might. It came with a cold crisp dill pickle spear and some of crunchy home made chips. The guy that took my order was cool and the woman that made the food was fast.  It's a good place to eat.</Text>

< text>
One of the best experiences and hidden gems withing Sonoma and Healdsburg.  I came here for the first time back in 2013 and loved it to much I knew I had to come back this year.  We briefly met one of the owner's Dawn at the event room and she quickly greeted us with a smile.  The tastings were being held at the tasting room that night and she gave us directions and wished us a happy tasting.  The ONLY reason I'm giving them 4 stars is because we arrived at the tasting room that night at 6:15pm and were told they were closed and finishing their last tasting.  I understand their tastings are intimate but we could've ran through the wines in 15 minutes easy.  Despite the minor issue we made it back around 4pm the next afternoon and had an amazing tasting with Tony and I ended up with yet another bottle of Ravish Melange (right bank Bordeaux replica.)  If you like french style reds that are age worthy DO NOT skip Williamson Wines.</text>

<rating>5<//rating><Review>Came here for a jazz event for the first time and let me tell you. It was a real treat. An intimate crowd setting with some great acoustics and sound mix paired with some of the best jazz musicians in all of Los Angeles. Unlike some of the bigger concert venues scattered throughout the city, this one was cozy and memorable, creating an atmosphere where the musicians can play and interact with the audience without pretense. We had an incredible time and will be back next month for the Jazz night! Was absolutely worth the drive down to San Pedro for such a treat. And getting the table seats in the rear is worth it. Better seats and better views! Only downside is that food is not served there, only a small pop-up bar, so eat beforehand and then come enjoy the music! Highly recommend it!<//Review><pictures>[{'url': ['https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/p/AF1QipNE5NBWKS0YbDhUfpkcXVyL9T2PUm5tpc4oUXiI=w150-h150-k-no-p']}, {'url': ['https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/p/AF1QipN4uMVKb8N0Un8ddHyPwFMyyKU_QRqh7_qXeUxo=w150-h150-k-no-p']}, {'url': ['https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/p/AF1QipPyU2_MWlv2l9llGEwbquf2srQlGwUR7UV50Ygl=w150-h150-k-no-p']}]<//pictures><response>None< /response>< gmap_id>

From the time you walk into the studio, which is clean and welcoming, you feel like you are a part of a community. Every staff member takes the time to get to know your name, and makes special efforts to make you feel like "part of the family". The Bar Method instructors are knowledgeable and guide you through every step of the class. The workout can be intense, and with the encouragement, hands on adjustment to your form, and the information you are given about why you are doing what you are doing, you push through the challenge and finish the hour feeling like you have really accomplished something. I am not a "gym person". I don't enjoy lifting heavy things, and I don't enjoy the gym atmosphere. The only workout routines that I have ever stuck with have been fun and encouraging. This fits the bill for me. I have been a member at Point Loma for more that a year. I go to 3-4 classes per week, and I never feel like it is a chore. I love the community, encouragement, and the physical and mental strength I have developed. I highly recommend this workout to anyone! I'm stronger than I have ever been and I owe it to the great staff at Bar Method Point Loma!!</text>

< review>
So, first off don't get me wrong the place has amazingly fresh seafood and a good selection of drinks and toppings. Also they are very ecco friendly if that sort of thing, is what strikes you. However now for the three stars. The prices are through the roof for a poke place. I went there around 4:30 pm. they were out of salmon and himachi....sigh. So my options were quite limited, so I went for the 3 scoops. I had tuna poke, spicy tuna and tako, AKA octopus, add an additional $3 for that. So for 3 scoops and a peach Tazo tea basically 30 bucks. So if your not affraid of the price check this place out. Otherwise there are plenty of less expensive options available.< /review>

All around amazing place to eat!< /review>
